Effective Date: 25 March 2004

Contact: Chanki Park ckp@nic.or.kr

Abstract

We submit 11,172 Hangul Syllables defined in Unicode 4.0 according to the consensus of Korean Internet community. Though most present computer environments support 11,172 Hangul Syllables submitted herein, some systems still support only 2,350 Hangul Syllables defined in KS X 1001:2002, which is a subset of 11,172 Hangul Syllables. These 2,350 syllables are asterisked in the comment line below. Thus, for the purpose of interoperability and stability, we recommend using 2,350 Hangul Syllables. Under the IETF IDN standards such as RFC 3490, 3491, and 3492, the registrar may inform registrants that other syllables except 2,350 syllables among the above 11,172 Hangul Syllables may not be supported.

Reference 1 KS X 1001:2002
Reference 2 Hangeul Syllables in Unicode 4.0
